msg:I went to Changsha with my friends for my birthday. The main purpose was to eat, drink and go shopping. I had my eyes on the Grand Hyatt with the best location, but the river view room was not cost-effective, so I chose Beichen Delta InterContinental as my second choice.
First of all, I would like to praise Ctrip! After booking, I communicated with Ctrip customer service to find out whether I could enjoy my InterContinental Platinum benefits on my birthday. The Ctrip lady was very nice. She asked for my membership number and asked for me. She said that except for membership points, InterContinental could arrange other needs depending on the situation on the day. Now Ctrip's service feels much better. They don't simply and rudely answer me with a general policy. They can really help customers solve problems. üåπ
Then I want to thank Fiona from InterContinental. She called me in advance to ask about my stay requirements. Because of my birthday and platinum membership, I was upgraded to a balcony room. When I checked out, because the cake was delivered late on the day of check-in (actually a small matter), she also gave me a very cute doll. üåπ
The location of this InterContinental is OK. It is quiet in the bustling city. It is very convenient to take a taxi to the main attractions. There are also many restaurants nearby. You can eat handmade rice noodles in the morning and walk to the ancient Kaifu Temple. It's quite comfortable. This balcony room only has a king-size bed. The bedroom area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe room feels very small, the balcony is also very small, and the bathroom space is very large. üòÇ The room I was given faces the landmark of the delta, but I feel that the night view will be more beautiful if it faces west. It is really comfortable to go back to the room and blow the wind in late April. There seems to be a KTV nearby at night, and you can hear it clearly even with the balcony door closed... Some people sang well, but some people shouted at the top of their voices, which was a bit overwhelming. My friend woke up laughing when she heard the singing while sleeping in bed üòÇ
This InterContinental can improve its room service~ There is no turndown service. Generally, InterContinental hotels will put my cosmetics in order when cleaning the room, but this one doesn't have it. But it's not a big problem!
The breakfast is also good~

msg:First of all, the hygiene is impeccable. I think InterContinental's hygiene is very good. It's unreasonable to say that the hygiene is not good at this price.
Let's talk about the environment. As shown in the picture, if you have expectations for this room, you will be disappointed when you enter. You can almost ignore the so-called river view. The design of this room is facing a building. You can see it clearly when you lie on the bed. Therefore, the curtains are almost closed. What river view can you expect from the window? Even if the window is open, people lying on the bed can only look at the building, and there is no scenery to speak of.
Let's talk about the service. For this kind of room, at least tell the customer. Remember that every time you check in at InterContinental Shenzhen OCT, the hotel will communicate the details of the room's distance from the elevator and the balcony, so that even if your room is full, the customer can understand it to some extent. However, the front desk of this handling has no communication about the details of the room throughout the whole process, and it can be said that there is no sense of service.
Overall, the price of 1599 is not recommended. There are more choices in Changsha at this price, and the originally high expectations have been reduced to the lowest.

name:Y‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçm‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçd‚Äçi‚Äçd‚Äçi

posted:Posted February 24, 2023
msg:Changsha Beichen InterContinental: After checking in for 2 hours, I decisively booked two more nights

advantage:
1. Invincible river view. First-line river view resources have always been precious. Beichen Intercontinental not only has a first-line river view, but also walks down the stairs to the riverside water fitness trail that stretches for several kilometers, completely unobstructed.
2. Casual and comfortable. It is not an exaggeration to say that we only decided where to stay when we got on the subway line 2 after arriving at Changsha South Railway Station. The tangled point is that almost all Changsha travel guides are recommending hotels within the Wuyi Square area, and they say that they go shopping when they go downstairs. But for us who defined this trip as a leisure trip, shopping is actually the difference between this street and that street. Therefore, the first choice is a reliable international chain hotel, clean and comfortable services are guaranteed, and there is a certain space for activities in the hotel, which is very important. After checking in, I found that the hardware and software (service) here were very satisfactory, so I decisively booked another two nights.
3. There is stillness in "wang". Don't get me wrong, the surrounding area of Beichen Intercontinental is not a tourist area, but it is definitely a good hotel for short-distance trips (3 days and 2 nights, 4 days and 3 nights) who like mid-to-high-end leisure life. Judging from the daily taxi records of online car-hailing, the fare from the hotel to all places around Wuyi Square does not exceed 20, and the time does not exceed 20 minutes, and it can be reached in 10 minutes at the fastest. That is, shopping" concerns. And next to the hotel is the Joy City Shopping Center. Every day from 10 am to 10 pm, the passage connecting the hotel will be open. It is no exaggeration to say that from the room to entering the mall, it only takes 3 minutes to wear pajamas. We tried one of the nights to watch a movie "No Name" at 10 o'clock, and it took only 5 minutes to walk back to the hotel after watching it at 12 o'clock. Lawson and Starbucks in Joy City basically meet the rigid needs of urban residents, and there are even two Cha Yan Yue Se, which is always used as the highlight of other hotel reservations. "Lu Ge Restaurant" is on the 4th floor of the Internet celebrity Changsha cuisine. If you are not used to spicy food, there are also Daoxiang and "Tai Er" that Cantonese people like. The "Blind" bookstore on the fifth floor is a new-style bookstore in the style of "Fangsuo" and "Shengpin". It is no problem at all to buy souvenirs and read books to pass the time. The key point is that there are all newly built high-end neighborhoods around here, and people who go shopping on non-weekends are not crowded, and there is basically no need to queue up to reserve a table for dinner.
4. The breakfast is great. Take a lazy sleep, eat a rich and delicious breakfast, and go shopping until 11 o'clock can save you a lunch. Beichen Intercontinental's buffet breakfast is a very important plus point for increasing happiness during this trip . To be honest, there is no shortage of ways to solve food and clothing in big cities, and I have long disliked eating buffets. But the buffet at Beichen InterContinental made me feel the caring and sincerity of being a five-star hotel. In addition to the standard varieties, there are authentic Changsha snacks and delicacies, including "ice powder", "sweet wine soy milk" and "suo powder". I don't comment on the taste, but at least tourists can find a little local in the same element. Secondly, there is actually a coffee bar here. The barista in the water bar uses the coffee machine to make all kinds of coffee equivalent to at least 15-20 yuan a cup outside, and watching everyone take a cup of coffee when they leave every day. A sense of identity? Furthermore, there are actually 5 kinds of tea (Pu'er, Tieguanyin, Jasmine...) available for fresh brewing. Isn't this more attentive than all "red teapots"? Moreover, red dates and walnut tea are freshly ground every day (I watched the little brother grind and smash it on the spot). I think at least the food and beverage director here has ulterior motives. Of course, I admit that I haven‚Äôt even left Guangzhou for three years due to the epidemic, so naturally I seldom eat breakfast in five-star hotels. If this is available at other Intercontinentals, I'm ignorant.

shortcoming:
In fact, before booking an Intercontinental, I will also read the bad reviews. But reading bad reviews also requires a little analytical ability. Some of them are obviously fault-finding or malicious slander, and everyone decides for themselves. But if I am forced to find shortcomings, I can give some suggestions for improvement based on the situations I have encountered or the facilities I have used.
1. The cafeteria provides tea, but no teapot. (feedback to restaurant manager)
2. The glass on the hotel's exterior wall is not reflective on one side. If you don't close the curtains, you can see it from the outside.
3. The passage connecting the hotel and the adjacent shopping mall closes too early. It is best if it can be arranged to close at 12 o'clock. In this way, at least the next time you watch a movie, you don't have to go outside to enter.

If the above shortcomings affect everyone's consideration for staying, then you should not live here.

Finally, let's talk about the price.

On non-weekends, I saw on Ctrip that there is a package with double breakfast for 3 days and 2 nights. The river view double bed room is 1999 yuan, and the separate room is 999 yuan (non-river view) but breakfast is not included. From personal experience, you can check whether you can upgrade the river view room for free according to the sales situation of the room.

The price is dynamic, so you can shop around, but the experience is a real evaluation, you can complain if you don‚Äôt like it, anyway, it will help me increase my popularity.

During the Spring Festival, we should understand each other. So this is not a complaint, but just expressing my feelings. I don't think I will come to Changsha on purpose in the future, and I hope to leave better services to future guests.
